<rating>4<//rating>< text>
Overall, the food was good. The Ahi tuna plate was very tasty and was cooked perfectly. The grilled corn was also very good, lots of flavor. I had the roasted veggies which were pretty good but nothing insanely special. The prices seem a little high for the salads but were what I expected for the tuna.

The decor leaves a little to be desired. The place feels almost too big and too white. The massive amount of powerful overhead fluorescents doesn't help. The Chipotle-style counter that you walk down seems tiny compared to the whole space.

I would go back, but I'd probably take it to go.< /text>

< text>
Worst moving experience in my life after 10+ moves. The moving team of three had only one person who seemed to know what they were doing. The others, as they wrapped and moved items, looked like it was their first time. All three were very slow - no hustle at all in comparison to watching other moving companies' employees. The move took over twice as long as was estimated (10 hours for a move with only a half hour drive between places, for a small 2BR apartment), thus was more than twice the cost to us.  They also broke two very sturdy pieces of furniture (a desk and a cat tree). The clincher was that, during a pandemic, I had to ask repeatedly for the movers to wear their masks appropriately. Wearing it on your chin or just over your mouth is not safe. Having our safety and our property both treated disrespectfully was unacceptable. The managers I followed up with was responsive and issued a full refund which we appreciated. Nevertheless I would absolutely recommend against hiring Pure Moving. I've attached below screenshots of the email I sent to them after the move was complete. They connected me to the emotionally infantile and unprofessional complete narcissist of a general manager, Frank Eady, who proceeded to flip flop between flattering me and screaming at me on the phone in response to me requesting a refund.

Normally I would have packed myself and just had people do the moving, but due to my hand disability, I needed help with the packing this time. As they did a terrible job, damaged things, lied, were disrespectful, and ultimately failed to complete the task of preventing me from having to pack and move things myself due to the disability, I requested a refund.

Hilariously, Frank accused me of trying to ruthlessly bankrupt a small family-owned business, as if I should feel bad for THEM because I requested a refund for a small job they did terribly and intentionally took several times as long as necessary for (thus upping the price), simply because they are a "small family owned business" trying to rip me off. <Date>1584993948960</Date><rate>5</rate>< review>
I worked with Max and his moving partner for a 1 bedroom in-city move and couldn't be happier with our experience.

From the beginning, the team at Pure Moving was responsive when I reached out for a quote. The booking process was painless and easy.

Max showed up right on time the weekend morning we planned to move, and now I'll try and rattle off the reasons we would definitely use Pure Moving company again for our next move:
- They found parking and immediately got to work. Parking at both locations was definitely something we were worried about, but Max assured us the parking he would handle, and handle it he did.
- They carefully wrapped fragile items (like our TV and bookcases) to be sure nothing was damaged during the move. Extremely professional with all the heavy and fragile items in our apartment.
- They brought tons of extra wrapping paper for fragile items that they let me use while I helped them box up items in the kitchen.
- They were great about checking which items should be packed into their boxes so we could keep track of everything for unpacking.
- They worked exceptionally hard all day long. They had to go up and down 2 flights of stairs on both ends of the move and they worked tirelessly all day long.
- Lastly, they were both extremely friendly, easy to talk to, and made the extremely difficult process of moving, much easier.

At the end of the move, we had Max and his moving partner for ~8 hours, which might have been longer than we initially expected, but we would definitely pick these guys again for any move because of their work ethic and professionalism.

Thanks again Max!< /review>

This was my first time using professional movers and I couldn't be happier choosing Pure Moving. I was moving from Oakland to San Mateo on my own which made me nervous, but JJ and Mark made the whole process smooth and efficient. <user>105582350533317498657<//user><Review>Awesome boba tea place. Love how they have fruit pieces as an option for add ons. Also they have a gigantic 32oz size which should be a standard size for other tea places.

One thing that they don't do is the vacuum seal on the cup though, which is a little annoying since it's harder to bike home with it in my backpack.

Update- I love this boba shop. I honestly love this place so much. I've had all of their teas on their menu and a few of the blended drinks. I enjoy the Strawberry Ecsteasy the most.

The boba though... Omfg...The first few times I've had the boba here, it was really good but nothing spectacular. Just a unique colored boba I thought. But the past few times I came here to get some drinks, the boba was on another level. I've never, ever, ever had boba like this in my entire life and I've consumed copious amounts of boba in my life. The consistency was like that of mochi, very soft and delicate yet bouncy and chewy like no other. Maybe they made it fresh right before I ordered it, but wow, I was so happy that I could have cried. It was life changing. I am a changed man now. Really.<//Review>< Rating>
5</Rating>
